self = <queue3.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7fe6ad6aa560>

    def removeAtTail(self):
    
        """Remove node at tail end."""
    
        if self.__size < 0:
            return None
        elif self.__size == 1:
            nodeToRemove = self.__tail
            nodeToRemove.prev = None
            self.__sentinel.next = None
            self.__head = self.__sentinel
            self.__tail = self.__sentinel
            self.__size -= 1
            return nodeToRemove
        else:
            nodeToRemove = self.__tail
            previous = nodeToRemove.prev
            nodeToRemove.prev = None
>           previous.next = None
E           AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'next'

    def removeAtTail(self):
